<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0"><font style="font-size: 25pt"><b>End Amazon&rsquo;s Unequal Vote-Counting</b></font></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.75in">To:</td><td>Amazon Shareholders</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.75in">Subject:</td><td><b>End unequal vote-counting practices that handicap shareholders </b></td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.75in">Action:</td><td><b>Vote FOR Proposal #15</b>, proxy page 38</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.75in">AGM:</td><td>May 22, 2019 @ 9:00am in Seattle, WA</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.75in">Contact:</td><td>Bruce Herbert, <font style="font-variant: small-caps">aif</font><br>
Investor Voice, <font style="font-variant: small-caps">spc</font><br>
team-at-investorvoice.net</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 6pt 0; text-align: center; font: 10pt Arial"><b>________________________________________</b></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 12pt Arial"><b>Fact:</b> Amazon uses two vote-counting formulas in its proxy.<sup>1</sup>
One favors reelection of Board members. The other formula undercounts support for shareholder-sponsored proposals (in a practice
known as &ldquo;formula-swapping&rdquo;). The difference lies in how <font style="font-variant: small-caps">abstain</font> votes
are counted.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="width: 80%; border-collapse: collapse;font: 10pt Arial">
<tr style="vertical-align: top">
    <td style="width: 9%">&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="width: 2%">&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="width: 39%; text-align: center"><p style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><font style="font-size: 9pt;font-family: Arial"><sup>(1)</sup>&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font style="font-size: 11pt;font-family: Arial">For
the Board Election:</font></p></td>
    <td style="width: 2%">&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="width: 7%">&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="width: 2%">&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="width: 39%; text-align: center"><p style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><font style="font-size: 9pt;font-family: Arial"><sup>(2)</sup>&nbsp;&nbsp;</font><font style="font-size: 11pt;font-family: Arial">For
Shareholder Items:</font></p></td></tr>
<tr style="vertical-align: top">
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="text-align: center"><font style="font: 12pt Arial"><b>Simple-Majority</b></font></td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="text-align: center"><font style="font: 12pt Arial"><b>Amazon&rsquo;s</b></font></td></tr>
<tr style="vertical-align: top">
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="text-align: center"><font style="font: 12pt Arial"><b>Formula</b></font></td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="text-align: center"><font style="font: 12pt Arial"><b>Formula</b></font></td></tr>
<tr style="vertical-align: top">
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="text-align: center">&nbsp;</td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="text-align: center"><font style="font-size: 10pt;font-family: Arial">vs:</font></td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="text-align: center">&nbsp;</td></tr>
<tr style="vertical-align: top">
    <td style="padding-left: 9pt; padding-bottom: 1pt"><font style="font: 9pt Arial">votes:</font></td>
    <td style="padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="text-align: center; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><font style="font: 12pt Arial"><b>FOR</b></font></td>
    <td style="padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="padding-bottom: 1pt">&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="text-align: center; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><font style="font: 12pt Arial"><b>FOR</b></font></td></tr>
<tr style="vertical-align: top">
    <td style="padding-left: 9pt; padding-bottom: 1pt"><font style="font: 9pt Arial">votes:</font></td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="text-align: center"><font style="font: 12pt Arial"><b>FOR + AGAINST</b></font></td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td>&nbsp;</td>
    <td style="text-align: center"><font style="font: 12pt Arial"><b>FOR + AGAINST <font style="color: blue">+ ABSTAIN</font></b></font></td></tr>
</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial"><b>Simple math:</b> When abstentions are added to the
denominator (i.e., below the line) it automatically reduces the final vote percentage. <b>This effectively stacks the deck</b>
against shareholders. It is unwarranted, and it harms shareholder best interest.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial"><b>A striking example:</b> At one company, a winning
<b>56.2%</b> simple-majority vote on proposed disclosure of political spending was transformed into a <b>34.2%</b> &ldquo;failing&rdquo;
vote (22 points lower) because the company employed formula-swapping. The company was Plum Creek Timber (PCL).<sup>2</sup></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial"><img src="page1_chart1.gif" alt=""></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>



<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 14pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>A.</b></td><td><b>Context for this Proposal</b></td></tr></table>



<div style="float: left; width: 48%; padding-right: 1%">

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>1.</b></td><td>Amazon&rsquo;s high-tech peers <b>Facebook</b>, <b>Apple</b>, and <b>Microsoft</b> count all shareholder votes using a fair,
simple-majority standard.</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.25in; text-indent: -0.25in;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>2.</b></td><td>Policy 3.7 of the <b>Council of Institutional Investors</b> (CII) declares that &ldquo;abstentions should be counted <u>only</u>
for purposes of a quorum&rdquo; (emphasis added).</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.25in; text-indent: -0.25in;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>3.</b></td><td><b>Institutional Shareholder Services</b> has written: &ldquo;ISS believes that a simple majority of voting shares should be
all that is necessary to effect change regarding a company and its governance provisions.&rdquo;</td></tr></table>


<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">

</div>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">

<div style="float: left; width: 48%; border: Black 1pt solid; padding-left: 1%">

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 12pt Arial"><b>Resolved</b>: Shareholders
ask the Board of Amazon.com, Inc. to take steps to amend Company governing documents to provide that all non-binding matters presented
by shareholders shall be decided by a simple majority of the votes cast FOR and AGAINST an item. This policy would apply to all
such matters unless shareholders have approved higher thresholds, or applicable laws or stock exchange regulations dictate otherwise.</p>

<p style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; margin-left: 0; text-indent: 0; text-align: left;font: 10pt Arial">

</div>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;<br style="clear: both">&nbsp;</p>


<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>4.</b></td><td>A Simple-Majority formula is mandated by the <b>U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission</b> (<b>SEC</b>) for use in determining
whether a proposal qualifies for resubmission.</td></tr></table>


<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">

<p style="margin: 6pt 0; text-align: center; font: 10pt Arial"><b><br>
________________________________________</b></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<div style="padding: 8pt; border: Black 1pt solid; background-color: rgb(220,230,242)">

<p style="margin: 0pt 0 0pt 4.3pt;font: 12pt Arial">The <b>Oxford English Dictionary</b></p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%;font: 10pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0.75in"></td><td style="width: 216pt; text-align: left; white-space: nowrap"><font style="font-size: 12pt; color: black">defines
                               <font style="font-variant: small-caps">Abstain</font> as: </font></td><td style="white-space: nowrap"><font style="font-size: 14pt; color: #984806"><b>To formally decline to vote
                                         </b><br>
                                         <b>either <font style="font-variant: small-caps">for</font> or <font style="font-variant: small-caps">against
                                         </font>a proposal or motion</b>.</font></td>
</tr></table>



</div>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 14pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>B.</b></td><td><b>Amazon Curtails Investor Choice</b></td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">With a <b>Simple-Majority standard </b>(only FOR and AGAINST
in the formula), investors have four possible choices when it comes to casting their ballot on a shareholder proposal:</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0.25in"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>1.</b></td><td style="width: 1.25in; white-space: nowrap"><p style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">Vote <b>FOR</b></p>
                                                                                </td>
    <td><p style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">= <u>ignoring</u> the Board&rsquo;s recommendation</p></td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0.25in"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>2.</b></td><td style="width: 1.25in"><p style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">Vote <b>AGAINST</b></p>

</td>
    <td>= <u>following</u> the Board&rsquo;s recommendation</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0.25in"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>3.</b></td><td style="width: 1.25in"><p style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">Vote <b>ABSTAIN</b></p>

</td>
    <td><p style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">= <u>neutral</u>, neither for nor against (as defined by the OED)</p>
</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0.25in"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>4.</b></td><td style="width: 1.25in"><p style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">Leave <b>blank</b></p>

</td>
    <td><p style="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">= Amazon votes it <u>following</u> the Board&rsquo;s recommendation</p>
</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">With a simple-majority standard, each of the three voting
options (besides leaving blank) is not only viable and unique, together they form a nuanced, meaningful, and distinct set of tools
for &lsquo;sending a message&rsquo;. These tools allow every investor to clearly signal intent.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">However, when Amazon includes abstentions in the formula
on shareholder proposals through formula-swapping, #3 can no longer be used to send a distinct message because it gets counted
in line with the Board&rsquo;s recommendation, just as #2 and #4 do.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">This diminishes the range of investor choice and further
tilts voting in Management&rsquo;s favor &ndash; all of which can happen without the shareholder ever being aware that votes are
being co-opted.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">Amazon&rsquo;s form of governance neglects voter intent
while limiting an investor&rsquo;s ability to send a clear message. This thwarts investor choice and harms shareholder best interest.<br style="clear: both">
</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2 -->
    <div style="margin-top: 8pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 2px solid"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><tr style="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><td style="width: 33%">&nbsp;</td><td style="width: 34%; text-align: center">&nbsp;</td><td style="width: 33%; text-align: right">&nbsp;</td></tr></table></div>
    <div style="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 8pt"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><tr><td style="text-align: right; width: 100%"><font style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;Amazon.com Exempt Solicitation | Page <!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->3<!-- Field: /Sequence --> of 4</font></td></tr></table></div>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 14pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>C.</b></td><td><b>Amazon Moots the Utility of an <font style="font-variant: small-caps">Abstain</font> Vote</b></td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">Shareholders can have many reasons to <font style="font-variant: small-caps">abstain</font>,
though often this involves seeking to &lsquo;send a message&rsquo; that the investor:</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0.25in"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>1.</b></td><td>Wants Management to pay close attention to the issue, signaling this by not following a Board recommendation to vote AGAINST.</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0.25in"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>2.</b></td><td>May like the proposal generally, but doesn&rsquo;t yet know enough to actively support it; or hasn&rsquo;t yet had time to
make the rounds of the institution to arrive at full buy-in.</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0.25in"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>3.</b></td><td>May look favorably on the proposal&rsquo;s core concept, but would like to see it expressed or implemented differently.</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0.25in"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>4.</b></td><td>Is genuinely agnostic and chooses to not register a vote.</td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">Regardless of an investor&rsquo;s intent, recharacterizing
all abstentions so as to offset FOR votes <u>eliminates</u> the <font style="font-variant: small-caps">abstain</font> vote&rsquo;s
utility. It advantages Board and Management, and it partially disenfranchises shareholders.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">Amazon&rsquo;s governance policy choices disadvantage
shareholders in two ways:</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0.5in"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><font style="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</font></td><td><font style="font-family: Arial">As detailed above, Amazon&rsquo;s use of formula-swapping effectively converts abstentions
into votes AGAINST any shareholder-sponsored proposal. </font></td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 12pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0.5in"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><font style="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</font></td><td><font style="font-family: Arial">Amazon&rsquo;s proxy stipulates that &ldquo;in the absence of directions&rdquo;
a returned ballot &ldquo;will be voted in accordance with the Board&rsquo;s recommendations&rdquo;.<sup>3</sup> Thus, when an
item is left blank, Management captures that vote. </font></td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">

<p style="margin: 6pt 0; text-align: center; font: 10pt Arial"><b>________________________________________</b></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt;font: 14pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 0.25in"><b>D.</b></td><td><b>Rebuttal to Amazon: Why Equal Vote-Counting Matters </b></td></tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">The Company&rsquo;s response<sup>4</sup> to this shareholder
Proposal includes a number of questionable and possibly misleading assertions. For example:</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 12pt Arial; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0pt"></td><td style="width: 90pt; text-align: left"><b>Misleading:</b></td><td><i>Amazon suggests that relatively small differences in
outcome are inconsequential</i>.</td>
</tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font: 12pt Arial; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; margin-left: 90pt; text-indent: 0pt">Due to formula-swapping, a number
of U.S. companies have undermined more than one hundred shareholder proposals.<sup>5</sup> These proposals earned a legitimate
majority vote under a simple-majority standard but were dismissed by the companies as having &ldquo;failed&rdquo; to pass.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font: 12pt Arial; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; margin-left: 90pt; text-indent: 0pt">A <u>majority</u> of these votes were subverted by an &ldquo;abstention
gap&rdquo; between the two formulas smaller than 4%.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 12pt Arial; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0pt"></td><td style="width: 90pt; text-align: left"><b>Misleading:</b></td><td><i>&ldquo;[Our] vote-counting methodology...does not inherently
favor proposals submitted by the Board over proposals submitted by shareholders.&rdquo;</i></td>
</tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font: 12pt Arial; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; margin-left: 90pt; text-indent: 0pt">The company&rsquo;s statement omits a crucial exception to the
rule: It is clear that Management&rsquo;s Board election proposal ignores abstentions (to the Board&rsquo;s benefit), while the
formula on shareholder items includes them (to shareholders&rsquo; detriment).</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 3 -->
    <div style="margin-top: 8pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 2px solid"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><tr style="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><td style="width: 33%">&nbsp;</td><td style="width: 34%; text-align: center">&nbsp;</td><td style="width: 33%; text-align: right">&nbsp;</td></tr></table></div>
    <div style="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 8pt"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><tr><td style="text-align: right; width: 100%"><font style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;Amazon.com Exempt Solicitation | Page <!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->4<!-- Field: /Sequence --> of 4</font></td></tr></table></div>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->


<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 12pt Arial; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0pt"></td><td style="width: 90pt; text-align: left"><b>Misleading:</b></td><td><i>&ldquo;[The Proposal&rsquo;s] methodology...would...disenfranchise...voters
who chose to abstain&rdquo;</i></td>
</tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font: 12pt Arial; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; margin-left: 90pt; text-indent: 0pt">As detailed above, the reality is that a simple-majority standard
<u>grants investors an additional option</u> for expressing intent &ndash; one that is eliminated under Amazon&rsquo;s chosen protocol.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 12pt Arial; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0pt"></td><td style="width: 90pt; text-align: left"><b>Misleading:<sup>&nbsp;&nbsp;</sup></b></td><td><i>Amazon implies its voting
                                         protocol is mandated by Section 216 of Delaware law</i>.<sup>6</sup></td>
</tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font: 12pt Arial; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; margin-left: 90pt; text-indent: 0pt">In fact, various options are available under Delaware law, not
just the one that Amazon employs. In stark contrast to being mandated, Amazon&rsquo;s protocol is the <u>least shareholder-friendly
approach permitted</u> under Delaware law.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 12pt Arial; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 0pt"></td><td style="width: 90pt; text-align: left"><b>Misleading:</b></td><td><i>Amazon states that the Proposal&rsquo;s request &ldquo;would
remove one of the voter&rsquo;s three options&rdquo;</i>.</td>
</tr></table>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font: 12pt Arial; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; margin-left: 90pt; text-indent: 0pt">In fact, a simple-majority standard not only allows <font style="font-variant: small-caps">abstain</font>
votes, it gives them a uniquely distinct meaning. This meaning is voided under Amazon&rsquo;s policy.</p>

<p style="margin: 6pt 0; text-align: center; font: 10pt Arial"><b>________________________________________</b></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0 0pt 67.5pt; text-indent: -67.5pt;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0 0pt 67.5pt; text-indent: -67.5pt;font: 14pt Arial"><b>Conclusion: Amazon&rsquo;s Double Standard</b></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">Companies understand that public perceptions count. It
is readily apparent, but not widely known, that Amazon employs a double standard. It stacks the voting deck against shareholders
in a way that makes it more difficult for shareholder proposals to succeed.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">Under a simple-majority standard, the <font style="font-variant: small-caps">abstain</font>
vote constitutes a real, distinct, and useful third choice for investors. It is a choice that delivers genuine message-sending
power.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in;font: 12pt Arial">Under Amazon&rsquo;s policy, however, the <font style="font-variant: small-caps">abstain</font>
vote is effectively eliminated and converted to be identical to two other options. These three options each benefit Management
by reducing the appearance of support for every issue raised by shareholders.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<div style="padding: 0in">

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center;font: 17pt Arial"><font style="font-variant: small-caps"><b>Therefore,</b></font></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center;font: 17pt Arial"><font style="font-variant: small-caps"><b>Please vote
FOR item #15</b></font></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center;font: 17pt Arial"><font style="font-variant: small-caps"><b>to end Unequal
Vote-Counting at Amazon</b></font></p>

</div>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center;font: 12pt Arial"><b>~ ~ ~</b></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify;font: 11pt Arial"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-variant: small-caps">Note: </font><font style="font-size: 10pt">This
is <u>not</u> a solicitation of authority to vote your proxy. Please DO NOT send us your proxy card; Investor Voice is <u>not
able</u> to vote your proxies, nor does this communication contemplate such an event. Investor Voice urges shareholders to <u>vote
FOR Item number 15</u> following the instructions provided on the management&rsquo;s proxy mailing.</font></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial"><u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</u></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt 0;font: 10pt Arial">&nbsp;</p>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 9pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">

outcome of the [Board] election&rdquo;; and &ldquo;For all other matters...[abstentions] are counted as present at the Annual Meeting
and entitled to vote&rdquo;.</td></tr></table>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; margin-top: 9pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 10pt Arial"><tr style="vertical-align: top">

for voting results related to the 5/11/05 AGM.</p>
